some of these reviews are absolutely unhinged</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2337155"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2337155#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2337134" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2337134" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="witchnextdoor"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1916685"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1916685.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="witchnextdoor" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2337134ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2337134" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1916685">witchnextdoor</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-03"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730682777" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bought this for a gorgeous man that I didn’t end up with, although we lasted much longer than the actual bottle. I LOVE sweet fragrances on men. This formula is really unique in that it’s smoky without being peppery; it’s smooth. (By the fireplace is my nightmare.) The exact opposite of that generic sharp/loud/spicy “mens cologne smell.” His chemistry may have been key lol. The vanilla, tobacco, sage, and rum mix is to die for. Just really gorgeous. Buy for a big warm man as a gift for yourself when you hug him.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2337134"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2337134#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2336957" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I guess that's true in the sense that this fragrance smells like someone just smoked a full pack of cigarettes and tried to cover it up with a vanilla perfume. /That/ perfume smells pretty good, but the cigarette is definitely not the type of tobacco/smokiness that I was looking for. I was very surprised to hate this scent, my friends--men and women alike--love it and recommended it to me when I asked for a tobacco, vanilla, boozy type scent. Bummer. <br />
<br />
No negative judgement on the price, sillage, longevity. Just the scent itself. ¯_(ツ)_/¯</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2336957"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2336957#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2336823" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; That is to say it’s got a quite masculine, aftershave/cologne splash heavy vibe that just doesn’t work for me. <br />
<br />
Cannot fathom the reviews that mention this being even remotely like By The Fireplace. The only note they share is the smoke. <br />
<br />
I definitely don’t think it’s a bad fragrance. And typically I have no problem wearing stuff geared towards masculine people. I wear Kouros, Ombre and Tuscan Leather, I wore Fahrenheit back in the early 2000s, Obsession for men, the list goes on. Jazz Club is just too much for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2336823"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2336823#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9); padding: 0; border: none; margin: 0;"><!-- Tag ID: fragranticacom_perfume_incontent_6 -->

It his you with a sweet, spicy and boozy goodness.  Slightly Smoky in a good way hard to describe.  It punches hard and a great fall/winter scent it is loud and the dry down takes its time which is great.  I think if it stayed the same as the top note it would be headache inducing after a few hours.  But they got it right, tones down to the tobacco and vanilla and vetiver notes with just right amount of rum scent.  It's a good one, try first and you will know if you like it or not quickly.  Only negative is it is almost too fruity sweet mixed in the rest.  Still good scent but as far as tobacco type scents, CK One for Him Shock is my favorite.  Even if you don't like CK, get a bottle of it $15.  It's a banger.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2336137"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2336137#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2334829" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1264910">seas13</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-28">10/28/24 10:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Oddly enough, the main note I get from this is the vetiver, even with all of the other aspects of the perfume. It’s a very mossy, river rock type smell. As it settles, very close to the skin I can pick up on the tobacco and rum, but overall it’s not as “boozy” as everyone describes. I actually love the mossy river rock smell which is specifically why I bought this fragrance even after smelling it though.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately, this fragrance has about zero longevity or sillage. It truly clings so close to the skin that you only really smell it on the skin and I feel that it doesn’t last more than 2-3 hours. This scent would probably do well layered with something; perhaps spraying this one on the skin at a few places like the neck that a significant other might smell it. Overall it needs a helping hand.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2330235"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2330235#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2329260" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2273768">joanofarc</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-23">10/23/24 18:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This feels like black tights. Late nights in Manhattan. A glossy blowout. Cigars and amber liquor. Jazz Club is a very fitting name.<br />
<br />
You can smell the booze and tobacco in the first spray, but it's matched evenly with the vanilla and neroli. Nothing feels overpowering - all the notes work together to strike a harmonious chord. This dries down to a sweet, rich scent with a ghost of its complexity. I actually think this fragrance suits women better, but I've yet to smell it on a man. TBD.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2325504"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2325504#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2325024" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868704">sharpteethstarlet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-16">10/16/24 21:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you ever half-passed out in a nicotine drenched taxi cab, after being basically kicked out of the bar at closing time - because the whiskey was just too good and the conversation with your date even better, you know what this smells like.<br />
<br />
I read some people find it too masculine and heavy, to me there’s hardly such a thing in perfumery. If this would be undeniably charming on a man, it would be absolutely divine on a woman that knows how to wear it.<br />
In terms of realism, it’s absolute perfection: it is both the interior of the most decadently beautiful jazz club, and the pungent, cold wind outside of it. Aromatic spiciness shields the warm, sweet cigarettes’ core.<br />
<br />
Wearing it, I feel like a sophisticated film noir detective in a trench coat, stepping on a carpet of crunchy red leaves in an autumn night. <br />
<br />
(@sharpteethstarlet on TT for more reviews 🌝)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2318264"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2318264#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318183" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not in a “im trying to convince myself to like it” way but I smelt it again a few months later and fell in love. It smelt so sensual and comforting. I then attained a sample size of it from my friend who hated it. I asked my friends what they think of it (all girls) and they HATE it. Say its too pungent, so if you’re looking for a mass appealing fragrance, this is not for you. On my skin, it smells amazing. Boozy tobacco scent. To be honest, if you don’t have a certain “aura” you can’t pull this off. Its definitely a mature scent but if you have the energy you can pull it off. Lasts around 6-7 hours on my skin. Wish the longevity and projection was better, but the scent makes up for it. DO NOT BLIND BUY!!! Chances are you won’t enjoy this. I am a girl who is more masculine and I LOVEEEEE THIS. <br />
<br />
Longevity 7/10<br />
Silliage 6.5/10 <br />
Scent 9/10<br />
Price 5.5/10<br />
<br />
Overall, if you have that certain vibe, like jazz music (ik it sounds absurd), like to dress in dark colors and hold yourself maturely go buy it (after smelling it)<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453">Fragrance_Nolan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 12:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Jazz Club is a simple fragrance that smells mostly like a tobacco cigar, especially in the opening. The vanilla and rum is present but it's very subtle and in the background. I think the scent gets better on the dry-down like a lot of people have been saying, as the tobacco fades and the vanilla and rum starts shining. The scent is really nice at that point. It is also mature-smelling, definitely a guy in his mid to late 20s and above. I can recommend this fragrance to someone only if they're a fan of the tobacco note, because it is present throughout the scent journey. I think Maison Martin Margiela did a good job in re-creating the scent of a jazz club, and I'm definitely a fan of the house after trying this fragrance. Jazz Club is an easy 9/10 for me, excellent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2313436"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2313436#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313182" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I’ve sampled Jazz Club multiple times and I think it is stunning, but there was always something about it that didn’t quite work for me. Today I realized what it was: the lavender that comes from the Clary Sage. Lavender is a note that my skin chemistry absolutely hates, even a perfectly nuanced hint of it (like you find in Jazz Club). This is an incredible fragrance, but one that you must test out on your skin before buying.<br />
<br />

This is probably because I live in a tropical country where it's hot 90% of the time and I have no occasion to wear this. I don't think this is a "compliment getter" though. This is one of those scents where it's either you make it your winter signature, or never wear it, if that makes sense. <br />
<br />
Scent 4/5<br />
Performance 2.5/5<br />
Price 3/5<br />
<br />
3.2/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2294706"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2294706#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294401" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2261073">theworldweknow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-21">09/21/24 15:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>i love this fragrance. the opening is predominantly smoky (someone who smelled it on me said it was very synthetic-y, however i disagree). it’s not a tobacco kind of smoky; it’s more of burning wood or incense smoke and i find it to be very pleasant despite how intense it is. as it dries down, the smokiness mellows and the sweet and boozy notes take the spotlight. unfortunately, i don't really smell any of the spiciness that some people describe this fragrance has. the projection is similar to most margiela fragrances, not intoxicating but also not weak. the longevity is also very typical of margiela, on skin this lasts 6 hours before becoming a skin scent. i believe this fragrance is great for fall and even winter due to it’s sweet and smokiness and i definitely recommend it. this scent is very unisex, i can see both men and women wearing this. in my opinion, this is a very attractive scent with well balanced notes that compliment each other perfectly. however, don’t blind buy it!!! the notes are very unique and sophisticated, because of that i advise you to test it out before committing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Then the incense dies down and I start getting creamy woody notes in the mid. The dry down is a ripe fruity, boozy, sandalwood.<br />
<br />
I can't be the only one that noticed the sandalwood in this, right?<br />
I know it's not listed as one of the notes, and I wasn't expecting it, but this to me is a sandalwood fragrance with some boozy and fruity aspects.<br />
<br />
I get hints of what I think may be the tobacco, but it's a synthetic smelling tobacco, akin to D&amp;G The One, and not a photorealistic tobacco like TF Tobacco Vanille.<br />
<br />
Good longevity, ok projection. Would make a nice cocktail party fragrance, or going out to a nice restaurant type vibe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2290006"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2290006#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288636" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2272507" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="beanna"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1698892"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="beanna" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2272507ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2272507" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1698892">beanna</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 09:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm confused by the 300 people comparing this to The One EDP. D&amp;G The One is one of my all-time favorite scents but I can't wear Jazz Club because of the intense smokiness. <br />
<br />
To my nose, Jazz Club is a completely different "sweet tobacco" style of fragrance than The One.<br />
While The One is a smooth blend of cardamom, amber, and cedar with an almost sweet tobacco leaf note in the background, the harsh and smokey tobacco in Jazz Club is front and center right from the first spray. If you are not a smoker, chances are you will find this tobacco/ashes note overpowering and cloying.<br />
The dry down is softer and becomes more inviting with the vanilla and vetiver, but 50% of the smell is still that of an ashtray throughout the life of the fragrance.<br />
The performance from my sample is fantastic. Strong projection and stays on clothes for more than 24 hours. I can still smell it radiating from my clothes from the day before when I step into the bathroom.<br />
<br />
Jazz Club smells exactly like its name and it's a commendable release by Maison Margiela worthy of the Replica moniker. Same impression with By the Fireplace. Extremely realistic, to a fault. But I simply can not see myself wearing this style of perfumery. As a non-smoker, I don't want to smell like an ashtray.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2272507"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2272507#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271870" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2263071" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="artemyst"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1490731"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="artemyst" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2263071ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2263071" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1490731">artemyst</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 17:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Was expecting to like this one, however the opening is much sweeter and more powdery than I was expecting from the notes. To my nose, vanilla takes the centre stage from the start accompanied by something powdery. It has a classic old-fashioned "perfume-y" accord, for want of a better expression. At one point during the opening I got the scent of caramelised sugar. The middle I like better and is more representative of the notes pyramid, however there is still something a little cloying about the scent that makes me just a little bit nauseous. It is a fairly office-friendly scent I think, the scent bubble being quite sweet and pretty clean. Keep in mind, my skin chemistry does often seem to amplify vanilla and sweet notes, so it could smell a little dirtier on others. <br />
I have a very sensitive nose (and am prone to headaches and nausea) so I tend to like fragrances that feel spacious and light, with not too much going on at once and the notes blending together quite seamlessly. This smells dense, with many separate notes simultaneously vying for dominance in a tight wrestling match. Ultimately, it feels like a perfume somewhat at war with itself; trying to portray a boozy speakeasy, but simultaneously trying to paper over the rough edges with powdery sweetness so as not to offend. But that's just my opinion as someone who likes a drier scent. <br />
Should appeal to those who likes a busier perfume with a lot of facets to find and experience; those who like a little tobacco/booziness but like it well-tempered by sweetness; and those who like an old-fashioned perfume. I'd probably find it pleasant enough on another person, but it's not for me and can be just slightly nauseating sniffed up close. To my nose and on my skin, it smells truly unisex, not masculine leaning.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2263071"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2263071#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2261789" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2208518">venusiangel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-31">07/31/24 18:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The first time I smelled this perfume I was in a sephora with my partner on the hunt for a new signature perfume, I'm a high femme who loves wearing a white floral vanilla amber type sweetness, but I've been wanting something more mature to match the sides of my personality that are more sensual and carnal. At first impression on a tester stick I found it a dismal let down from all the hype it had been receiving, especially because I am found of perfumery as an art in storytelling so the replica line immediately caught my interest. I found it a step up from By The Fireplace which I journaled smelled "like matches. straight @ss", but also stated it grew on me. Now I'm a huge jazz lover, so I wanted to love this a lot and admittedly, I had smelled way too much the first time I encountered this scent. So yesterday I went to try it on my wrist properly to give it a chance and had such an opposite reaction.<br />
Marketed as a unisex fragrance, though here it states masculine, I love this most as a women's perfume. Deeply provocative and empowering. So visceral I can smell the remnants of a cigar on a cheetah print faux fur coat sling over a bar chair. The smell of leather is wafting through the perfume on this olfactory journey through a manhattan jazz lounge. It smells like a sleazy man...and a really sexy dom femme. Yes I would hate to smell this on a man but it makes me feel like The Man™️ (tho I'm still unemployed). It gives S/S 1995 Mugler Couture, deep brick red lipstick, leather upholstery at the bar on a steamy date. This fragrance made me realize how much I like pink pepper as well, having to look up what note was tickling my nose throughout the life of the perfume. Sillage and longevity is nothing too crazy and I'm sure there's dupes in men's cologne somewhere, but for the marketing angle of bottling a memory in a fragrance...I'm deeply inspired and moved by the art of it all. Never smelt the neroli but definitely got that smooth booziness of the rum in a way that didn't feel cliche, maybe because I find it unconventional and unique on me, and sweet even. A little goes a long way this fragrance and I highkey would love a decant or small version of this perfume (someone gift it to me &lt;3)<br />
<br />
In conclusion: addictive, evocative, sensual. My mom said it smells like cheap men's cologne but there's something slightly androgynous and dominating and exciting about it in a way that can still read feminine. 8/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1985918">reneemaarja</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-19">07/19/24 09:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was one of the first 'grown-up' fragrances I ever bought and one I keep returning to for a reason. It's warm, a bit smoky, sweet but not cloying, and has a beautiful sparkle of pink pepper in the opening. I'm really sensitive to vanilla in fragrances but this does it so beautifully. Though this is marketed as masculine, I think this is really beautiful on women- it doesn't have the cutting cedar note present in a lot of MEN'S fragrance, yet has a very alluring androgyny to it. I'm not a fan of the other, 'darker' Margiela fragrances because I think their dry down is a bit sickly but this one is gorgeous from start to finish. Coming back to it after not wearing it for a while feels like coming home, gonna be re-purchasing this for a while.<br />
Edit: wanted to come back to this and say that I've seen some people complain about the longevity of Jazz Club- not really sure why they would, I can smell it on hoodies and sweaters for MONTHS after wearing them (and I don't spray this liberally). Maybe men are used to fragrances that you need to scrub off with bleach and lye but for most women, this one performs like crazy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2223410"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2223410#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2223182" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2223182" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Cosmos_PMF"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2108424.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Cosmos_PMF" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Xerjoff/Torino22-77059.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.77059.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Torino22"title="Torino22"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2223182ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2223182" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424">Cosmos_PMF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-19">07/19/24 04:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the "fall/autumn in a bottle" fragrance. It's also an entire journey to wear it. <br />
<br />
If I could name the entire smell of this cologne, it would be "majestic". It's very seductive <br />
<br />
It has a special rum note which differentiates the scent profile from the basic tobacco+vanilla combination of winter fragrances. <br />
It's boozy, sweet, natural tobacco smelling. Not exactly gourmand. The opposite of fresh, anyway. <br />
Once you escaped the alcohol-ish booziness of this fragrance (which is actually very pleasant and unique) you're gonna be travelled into the dry down which is absolutely sexy, dry edible vanilla with strong tobacco undertones.<br />
<br />
The performance on this is like a date night scent, 6-7hrs longevity with soft to moderate projection<br />
<br />
Talking about versatility, evening, night outs and dates during fall/autumn or winter, but of course there are gonna be some people choosing this in warm nights too. <br />
<br />
The bottle looks cute with the details of the fragrance written on a glued printed nice texture sheet, you can clearly see how much juice is left from the fragrance too<br />
The atomizer is average but I don't like the fact that this doesn't have a cap, a creative cap design for the entire Replica line. I'd leave this in a drawer during the heat weather so the juice inside it will last longer. <br />
<br />
Maison Margiela Replica Jazz Club: for sure the best from the brand, seductive asf, tobacco sweet boozy, niche line. Addictive. If you wanna have a 2 fragrances only collection, get a fresh/blue fragrance and this one. 9.25/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2223182"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2223182#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222390" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; More like La La Land on Netflix whilst eating rum and raisin ice cream. Theres a funny (unintentionally so) YT video where the reviewer wanders round a public park asking random ladies what they think of this.  Ratings given are generally in the 6-7/10 range.  To be fair he finds an enthusiastic reponse or two but the mildly positives outweigh the enthusiasts about five to one.  Said reviewer then professes Jazz Club to be a 'certified ladykiller'.  What nonsense.  This is decent, opens with a blast of booze (the good bit) then dries to a sort of dusty vanilla (meh).  Performance is just about okay and generally this is available on discount. Fair play if you like this sort of thing.  But a like not a love for me, just be wary of the hype, there are many better boozy tobacco fragrances around.   3/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2222390"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2222390#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2221947" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; For some reason, I thought this was one of Replica's unisex fragrances, but I'd say it's definitely masculine. Or maybe I was so looking forward to the Clary Sage, Neroli, and Lemon, that I disregarded the Tobacco Leaf and Rum (even though those notes perfectly explain why it's called Jazz Club!) Anyway, where I might really like smelling this on another person (despite not liking smoky smells, at all), it's not for me. Not horribly smoky. Definitely pleasant enough.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2218078"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2218078#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2217659" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was hoping for a more tobacco and vanilla dominated scent, but I'll still try and wear this to see how it behaves on skin. <br />
Update: after trying on skin, it definitely mellows out a lot. I'm not in love but easily wearable for me. The longevity seems okay, in an hour or so it's sitting close to the body but still noticeable. Unless it's been sprayed on fabric, then it's way more powerful and takes hours and hours for those top notes to fade. Overall an interesting scent, I'll probably be layering it with a musky vanilla in the future.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2216721"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2216721#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2216443" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Gris performs much better.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2211998"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2211998#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2208446" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2187574" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="glassbiome"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1885819"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1885819.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="glassbiome" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Scout-Dixon-West/Incarnate-97236.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.97236.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Incarnate"title="Incarnate"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2187574ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2187574" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1885819">glassbiome</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-13">06/13/24 20:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Jazz Club will always hold a special place in my heart for being my first full-bottle buy as well as introducing me the wonderful and exciting world of fragrance. All of my perfume experience was limited to celebrity body sprays and paper strips in magazines. Nothing interested me and at one point I believe I even said out loud "all perfume smells the same." This is not to say that Jazz Club is the exception or that it's uniquely perfect. Just that I was a silly child. And now I long for smoky lounges, spiced rum, vanilla tobacco and saxophone. I haven't been to a real life jazz club like many of the reviewers here, but the delicious, rich, glowing amber that JC embodies turns my bed room into one any night I want. It pairs and layers so well with so much. Lasts long, but doesn't overstay its welcome. Radiates enough to make you stand out in a room and feels so timeless and dynamic it suits any season, mood, or occasion. Really worth a shot even if everyone and their grandmother claims this as their signature scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="2187574"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=2187574#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2187377" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1153104" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1153104" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="lu.yves.katz"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173013"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1173013.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="lu.yves.katz" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Carthusia/1681-11494.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.11494.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="1681"title="1681"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1153104ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1153104" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173013">lu.yves.katz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-03-08">03/08/20 05:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As a musicologist and perfume fan I ordered my sample with high hopes, but I have to say, that I am rather disappointed. I tested it with a friend of mine who's a jazz bass player, because I thought it would be a funny idea.<br />
<br />
To my nose the intro of jazz club is mainly sweet in a one dimensional and obnoxious way. Think bright, sweet vanillin instead of dark and sweet actual vanilla pods.<br />
After 30 minutes me and my friend noticed a sharp and slightly alcoholic scent, that reminded me of shaving foam and my friend of lynx deodorant (Axe as it's called in Germany). With the artificial sweetness and the lynx came along the headache and nausea I experienced in my teen years, whenever someone in school wore a liter of Axe. Do people still wear that stuff? Or does it still smell that way? <br />
<br />
I was completely baffled and considered, if perhaps my nose was having a bad day, but scrolling through the comments here, I realized, that other people had the same association. Jazz Club unfortunately doesn't work at all for me and my friend. I was told by my friend that I should mention, that "this is the smell, that someone who has never been to a jazz club imagines a jazz club to smell.".</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="1153104"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=1153104#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent979507" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc979507" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="C-Sauce"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090845"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1090845.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="C-Sauce" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma979507ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd979507" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090845">C-Sauce</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-09-07">09/07/18 02:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I find that this scent makes me feel depressed. It reminds me of the smell of my jacket the morning after a drunken bringe. I used to drink Appleton rum and smoke cigarettes at a friend’s place into the small hours. The smell of booze spilt on my clothes and skin the next day was often enough to put me on the wagon for at least a couple of days. I don’t understand why anyone would want to smell like an alcoholic. To me it literally triggers flashbacks of brutal hangovers.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="979507"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=979507#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1621188" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1621188" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="dpark"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1516832"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1516832.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="dpark" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1621188ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1621188" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1516832">dpark</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-10">08/10/22 19:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Experience:  Chainsmoking aunt is wearing Spicebomb.<br />
<br />
I get smoke, powder, tobacco, plus a little spice and vanilla. I don’t pick up the rum or much of anything else, but the smoke obscures a lot.<br />
<br />
The smoke makes the whole thing sort of gritty or edgy. It also kind of ruins the whole thing for me. I understand the scent combo they’re going for, but I’d much rather a jazz club in a city that has banned indoor smoking.<br />
<br />
If you don’t mind (or even prefer) a bit of smoke in your fragrance and you want that warm spicy feel, you’ll probably love this. If you don’t like smoke at all, I’d recommend steering clear.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="1621188"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=1621188#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1208611" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1208611" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="yager"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249819"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="yager" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1208611ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1208611" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249819">yager</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-08-07">08/07/20 09:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>At first I found Jazz Club quite funny. It smelt a lot like a high end version of a lynx antiperspirant that I used when I was kid combined with the smell they pipe into the dungeon museum near where I live. I weirdly liked it. <br />
<br />
A few hours and a couple of wrist scrubbings later and it's still there and now smells exactly like the lynx spray. I'm trapped in my teenage years and it's definitely not funny any more.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="20541"comment_id="1208611"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/Jazz-Club-20541.html?ccid=1208611#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1762548" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; On my skin i only get nondescript artificial fruit spun into cotton candy mixed with an extremely ashy tobacco. It turned my stomach enough that I needed to scrub it off after 45 minutes.                 if (lang == 'UK') $("a.en2inter").attr("href", function () {
            return this.href.replace(/www.fragrantica.com/, "www.fragrantica.ua").replace(/perfume/, "perfumes") });
                if (lang == 'MN') $("a.en2inter").attr("href", function () {
            return this.href.replace(/www.fragrantica.com/, "www.fragrantica.mn").replace(/perfume/, "perfumes") });
                if (lang == 'HE') $("a.en2inter").attr("href", function () {
            return this.href.replace(/www.fragrantica.com/, "www.fragrantica.co.il").replace(/perfume/, "perfumes") });
            });
</script>

    if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
        // Use the window load event to keep the page load performant
        window.addEventListener('load', () => {
            navigator.serviceWorker.register('/service-worker.js?v=rtgK1d3eddb45a054fd62fdca9a01c72fbac6');
        });
    }
</script>
